kinzalmono belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . they work by causing the blood vessels to narrow , causing your blood pressure to rise . kinzulmono blocks the activity of the hormone that makes your blood vessels relax . this helps to lower the blood pressure . it is used to treat essential hypertension ( high blood pressure) in adults . the highblood pressure can damage blood vessels in several organs , such as heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness .

ninlaro is used for the treatment of multiple myeloma . this medicine contains the active substance lenalidomide . it is a medicine called dexamethasone , which is an anti - inflammatory medicine . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you start . you will be given a dose of nilaro once a day , once , twice a week for the first 3 weeks . lenlaride is used in combination with lenalidomide and dexaliosone . the other ingredients are : - it is used to treat a single dose of 25 mg . first doses of lenalidose is given once every 4 weeks for the second week of the first week of treatment .
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . very common serious side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) low platelet counts ( thrombocytopenia ), nose bleeds , easily bruise nausea , vomiting , diarrhoea , numbness or tingling , burning of the hands or feet ( peripheral neuropathy ), swelling of the legs or feet , peripheral oedema ), skin rash or itchy in the body . rare side effects may affect more than 1 in 1 , 000 people . ninlaro can cause a number of side effects not known . this includes any possible side effect not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v .

zerene contains the active substance benzodiazepine , which belongs to a group of medicinal products called hypnotic actions . it is used to treat sleeping problems after treatment . treatment should be stopped if you have problems sleeping .
